:i function $tod_manager_set_default_params$
	:i $GetLevelStructureName$
	:i $FormatText$$ChecksumName$ = $level_tod_morning_params$%s(21,"%a_tod_morning_params")$a$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_structure_name$->$level$) 
	:i $FormatText$$ChecksumName$ = $level_tod_day_params$%s(23,"%a_tod_afternoon_params")$a$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_structure_name$->$level$) 
	:i $FormatText$$ChecksumName$ = $level_tod_evening_params$%s(21,"%a_tod_evening_params")$a$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_structure_name$->$level$) 
	:i $FormatText$$ChecksumName$ = $level_tod_night_params$%s(19,"%a_tod_night_params")$a$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_structure_name$->$level$) 
	:i $FormatText$$ChecksumName$ = $level_tod_alt_params$%s(17,"%a_tod_alt_params")$a$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_structure_name$->$level$) 
	:i if NOT $GotParam$$morning_params$
		:i if $GlobalExists$$name$ = %GLOBAL%$level_tod_morning_params$$type$ = $structure$
			:i $printf$%s(35,"## using custom level tod values!!!")
			:i $morning_params$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_tod_morning_params$) 
		:i else 
			:i $morning_params$ = $tod_manager_default_morning$
		:i endif
	:i endif
	:i if NOT $GotParam$$afternoon_params$
		:i if $GotParam$$use_alternate_default_params$
			:i if $GlobalExists$$name$ = %GLOBAL%$level_tod_alt_params$$type$ = $structure$
				:i $printf$%s(35,"## using custom level tod values!!!")
				:i $afternoon_params$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_tod_alt_params$) 
			:i else 
				:i $afternoon_params$ = $tod_manager_default_afternoon$
			:i endif
		:i else 
			:i if $GlobalExists$$name$ = %GLOBAL%$level_tod_day_params$$type$ = $structure$
				:i $printf$%s(35,"## using custom level tod values!!!")
				:i $afternoon_params$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_tod_day_params$) 
			:i else 
				:i $afternoon_params$ = $tod_manager_default_afternoon$
			:i endif
		:i endif
	:i endif
	:i if NOT $GotParam$$evening_params$
		:i if $GlobalExists$$name$ = %GLOBAL%$level_tod_evening_params$$type$ = $structure$
			:i $printf$%s(35,"## using custom level tod values!!!")
			:i $evening_params$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_tod_evening_params$) 
		:i else 
			:i $evening_params$ = $tod_manager_default_evening$
		:i endif
	:i endif
	:i if NOT $GotParam$$night_params$
		:i if $GlobalExists$$name$ = %GLOBAL%$level_tod_night_params$$type$ = $structure$
			:i $printf$%s(35,"## using custom level tod values!!!")
			:i $night_params$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_tod_night_params$) 
		:i else 
			:i $night_params$ = $tod_manager_default_night$
		:i endif
	:i endif
	:i $TODManager_SetParams$:s{
		:i $system$ = %i(1,00000001)
		:i $current_state$ = $afternoon$
		:i $transition_length$ = %i(90000,00015f90)
		:i $groups$ = :a{
			:i :s{$parts$ = %i(6,00000006)$wait_frames$ = %i(3,00000003)$light_group$ = $outdoor$:s}
			:i :s{$parts$ = %i(2,00000002)$wait_frames$ = %i(3,00000003)$light_group$ = $nolevellights$$reset_light_group$ = $indoor$:s}
			:i :a}
		:i $morning$ = %GLOBAL%$morning_params$
		:i $afternoon$ = %GLOBAL%$afternoon_params$
		:i $evening$ = %GLOBAL%$evening_params$
		:i $night$ = %GLOBAL%$night_params$
	:i :s}
	:i $TODManager_SetParams$:s{
		:i $sky$
		:i $system$ = %i(2,00000002)
		:i $current_state$ = $afternoon$
		:i $transition_length$ = %i(90000,00015f90)
		:i $groups$ = :a{
			:i :s{$parts$ = %i(6,00000006)$wait_frames$ = %i(3,00000003)$light_group$ = $outdoor$:s}
			:i :s{$parts$ = %i(2,00000002)$wait_frames$ = %i(3,00000003)$light_group$ = $nolevellights$$reset_light_group$ = $indoor$:s}
			:i :a}
		:i $morning$ = %GLOBAL%$morning_params$
		:i $afternoon$ = %GLOBAL%$afternoon_params$
		:i $evening$ = %GLOBAL%$evening_params$
		:i $night$ = %GLOBAL%$night_params$
	:i :s}
	:i if $StructureContains$$structure$ = %GLOBAL%$morning_params$$sun_theta$
		:i $Change$$morning_sun_theta$ =  (%GLOBAL%$morning_params$->$sun_theta$) 
		:i $Change$$morning_sun_phi$ =  (%GLOBAL%$morning_params$->$sun_phi$) 
		:i $Change$$morning_sun_red$ =  (%GLOBAL%$morning_params$->$sun_red$) 
		:i $Change$$morning_sun_green$ =  (%GLOBAL%$morning_params$->$sun_green$) 
		:i $Change$$morning_sun_blue$ =  (%GLOBAL%$morning_params$->$sun_blue$) 
	:i else 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_theta$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_morning$) ->$sun_theta$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_phi$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_morning$) ->$sun_phi$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_red$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_morning$) ->$sun_red$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_green$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_morning$) ->$sun_green$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_blue$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_morning$) ->$sun_blue$) 
	:i endif
	:i if $StructureContains$$structure$ = %GLOBAL%$afternoon_params$$sun_theta$
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_theta$ =  (%GLOBAL%$afternoon_params$->$sun_theta$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_phi$ =  (%GLOBAL%$afternoon_params$->$sun_phi$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_red$ =  (%GLOBAL%$afternoon_params$->$sun_red$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_green$ =  (%GLOBAL%$afternoon_params$->$sun_green$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_blue$ =  (%GLOBAL%$afternoon_params$->$sun_blue$) 
	:i else 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_theta$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_afternoon$) ->$sun_theta$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_phi$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_afternoon$) ->$sun_phi$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_red$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_afternoon$) ->$sun_red$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_green$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_afternoon$) ->$sun_green$) 
		:i $Change$$afternoon_sun_blue$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_afternoon$) ->$sun_blue$) 
	:i endif
	:i if $StructureContains$$structure$ = %GLOBAL%$evening_params$$sun_theta$
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_theta$ =  (%GLOBAL%$evening_params$->$sun_theta$) 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_phi$ =  (%GLOBAL%$evening_params$->$sun_phi$) 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_red$ =  (%GLOBAL%$evening_params$->$sun_red$) 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_green$ =  (%GLOBAL%$evening_params$->$sun_green$) 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_blue$ =  (%GLOBAL%$evening_params$->$sun_blue$) 
	:i else 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_theta$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_evening$) ->$sun_theta$) 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_phi$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_evening$) ->$sun_phi$) 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_red$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_evening$) ->$sun_red$) 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_green$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_evening$) ->$sun_green$) 
		:i $Change$$evening_sun_blue$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_evening$) ->$sun_blue$) 
	:i endif
	:i if $StructureContains$$structure$ = %GLOBAL%$night_params$$sun_theta$
		:i $Change$$night_sun_theta$ =  (%GLOBAL%$night_params$->$sun_theta$) 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_phi$ =  (%GLOBAL%$night_params$->$sun_phi$) 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_red$ =  (%GLOBAL%$night_params$->$sun_red$) 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_green$ =  (%GLOBAL%$night_params$->$sun_green$) 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_blue$ =  (%GLOBAL%$night_params$->$sun_blue$) 
	:i else 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_theta$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_night$) ->$sun_theta$) 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_phi$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_night$) ->$sun_phi$) 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_red$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_night$) ->$sun_red$) 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_green$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_night$) ->$sun_green$) 
		:i $Change$$night_sun_blue$ =  ( ($tod_manager_default_night$) ->$sun_blue$) 
	:i endif
:i endfunction
:i function $tod_manager_get_tod_new_strings$
	:i switch %GLOBAL%$next_tod$
		:i case $morning$
			:i $next_tod_string$ = %s(7,"Morning")
			:i endcase
		case $afternoon$
			:i $next_tod_string$ = %s(3,"Day")
			:i endcase
		case $evening$
			:i $next_tod_string$ = %s(7,"Evening")
			:i endcase
		case $night$
			:i $next_tod_string$ = %s(5,"Night")
			:i endcase
		default 
			:i $next_tod_string$ = %s(3,"Day")
			:i end_switch
	
	:i switch  ($tod_current_state$) 
		:i case $morning$
			:i $current_tod_string$ = %s(7,"Morning")
			:i endcase
		case $afternoon$
			:i $current_tod_string$ = %s(3,"Day")
			:i endcase
		case $evening$
			:i $current_tod_string$ = %s(7,"Evening")
			:i endcase
		case $night$
			:i $current_tod_string$ = %s(5,"Night")
			:i endcase
		default 
			:i $current_tod_string$ = %s(3,"Day")
			:i end_switch
	
	:i $Change$$tod_current_state$ = %GLOBAL%$next_tod$
	:i return
	$current_tod_string$ = %GLOBAL%$current_tod_string$$next_tod_string$ = %GLOBAL%$next_tod_string$
:i endfunction
:i function $tod_manager_state_transition$
	:i $Change$$TOD_CHANGE_IS_DONE$ = %i(0,00000000)
	:i $SpawnScript$$tod_manager_update_car_textures$$params$ =  isNull 
	:i $GetLevelStructureName$
	:i $tod_manager_get_tod_new_strings$ isNull 
	:i $FormatText$$TextName$ = $level_tod_transition_name$%s(13,"%a_TOD_%bTo%c")$a$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_structure_name$->$level$) $b$ = %GLOBAL%$current_tod_string$$c$ = %GLOBAL%$next_tod_string$
	:i $FormatText$$ChecksumName$ = $level_tod_transition_script$%s(13,"%a_TOD_%bTo%c")$a$ =  (%GLOBAL%$level_structure_name$->$level$) $b$ = %GLOBAL%$current_tod_string$$c$ = %GLOBAL%$next_tod_string$
	:i $printf$%s(30,"level_tod_transition_name = %a")$a$ = %GLOBAL%$level_tod_transition_name$
	:i $printf$%s(30,"level_tod_transition_name = %a")$a$ = %GLOBAL%$level_tod_transition_name$
	:i $printf$%s(30,"level_tod_transition_name = %a")$a$ = %GLOBAL%$level_tod_transition_name$
	:i if $GotParam$$level_tod_transition_script$
		:i if $ScriptExists$%GLOBAL%$level_tod_transition_script$
			:i $SpawnScript$%GLOBAL%$level_tod_transition_script$
		:i endif
	:i endif
	:i $TODManager_GetCurrentTODParams$
	:i if $GotParam$$tod_params$
		:i $set_level_lights$%GLOBAL%$tod_params$
		:i if  ( (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom_on$)  = %i(1,00000001)) 
			:i $ScreenFx_SetBloomParams$:s{
				:i $On$
				:i $Threshold$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom1$) 
				:i $Strength$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom2$) 
				:i $Red$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom_color$:a{%i(0,00000000):a}) 
				:i $Green$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom_color$:a{%i(1,00000001):a}) 
				:i $Blue$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom_color$:a{%i(2,00000002):a}) 
			:i :s}
			:i $Change$$bloom_threshold$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom1$) 
			:i $Change$$bloom_strength$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom2$) 
			:i $Change$$bloom_r$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom_color$:a{%i(0,00000000):a}) 
			:i $Change$$bloom_g$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom_color$:a{%i(1,00000001):a}) 
			:i $Change$$bloom_b$ =  (%GLOBAL%$tod_params$->$bloom_color$:a{%i(2,00000002):a}) 
		:i else 
			:i $ScreenFx_SetBloomParams$$Off$
		:i endif
	:i endif
	:i if $GotParam$$set_inactive$
		:i $TODManager_SetActive$%i(0,00000000)
	:i else 
		:i $TODManager_SetActive$%i(1,00000001)
	:i endif
	:i $wait$%i(2,00000002)$gameframes$
	:i $Change$$TOD_CHANGE_IS_DONE$ = %i(1,00000001)
:i endfunction
:i function $tod_manager_update_car_textures$
	:i switch %GLOBAL%$next_tod$
		:i case $morning$
			:i $ReplaceCarTextures$:s{
				:i $array$ = :a{
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(31,"JKU_LightCircle_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(41,"textures/cars/JKU_LightCircle_Transparent")
					:i :s}
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(33,"JKU_HeadlightGlow_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(31,"textures/cars/JKU_HeadlightGlow")
					:i :s}
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(33,"JKU_TaillightGlow_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(31,"textures/cars/JKU_TaillightGlow")
					:i :s}
					:i :a}
			:i :s}
			:i endcase
		case $afternoon$
			:i $ReplaceCarTextures$:s{
				:i $array$ = :a{
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(31,"JKU_LightCircle_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(41,"textures/cars/JKU_LightCircle_Transparent")
					:i :s}
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(33,"JKU_HeadlightGlow_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(43,"textures/cars/JKU_HeadlightGlow_Transparent")
					:i :s}
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(33,"JKU_TaillightGlow_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(43,"textures/cars/JKU_TaillightGlow_Transparent")
					:i :s}
					:i :a}
			:i :s}
			:i endcase
		case $evening$
			:i $ReplaceCarTextures$:s{
				:i $array$ = :a{
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(31,"JKU_LightCircle_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(41,"textures/cars/JKU_LightCircle_Transparent")
					:i :s}
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(33,"JKU_HeadlightGlow_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(31,"textures/cars/JKU_HeadlightGlow")
					:i :s}
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(33,"JKU_TaillightGlow_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(31,"textures/cars/JKU_TaillightGlow")
					:i :s}
					:i :a}
			:i :s}
			:i endcase
		case $night$
			:i $ReplaceCarTextures$:s{
				:i $array$ = :a{
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(31,"JKU_LightCircle_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(29,"textures/cars/JKU_LightCircle")
					:i :s}
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(33,"JKU_HeadlightGlow_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(31,"textures/cars/JKU_HeadlightGlow")
					:i :s}
					:i :s{
						:i $src$ = %s(33,"JKU_TaillightGlow_Transparent.png")$dest$ = %s(31,"textures/cars/JKU_TaillightGlow")
					:i :s}
					:i :a}
			:i :s}
			:i endcase
		default 
			:i $printf$%s(18,"### no tod set ###")
			:i end_switch
	
:i endfunction
:i function $thugpro_change_time_of_day$
	:i $printf$%s(33,"script thugpro_change_time_of_day")
	:i $printf$%s(14,"tod_state = %a")$a$ = %GLOBAL%$tod_state$
	:i $printf$%s(20,"LEVEL_TOD_STATE = %a")$a$ =  ($LEVEL_TOD_STATE$) 
	:i $Change$$tod_manager_inactive$ = %i(0,00000000)
	:i $TODManager_SetActive$%i(1,00000001)
	:i $SpawnScript$$thugpro_tod_level_specific_hack_before$
	:i switch %GLOBAL%$tod_state$
		:i case $afternoon$
			:i $Change$$LEVEL_TOD_STATE$ = $afternoon$
			:i $TODManager_SetTODInstant$$afternoon$
			:i $set_current_tod_values$$tod_state$ = $afternoon$
			:i endcase
		case $night$
			:i $Change$$LEVEL_TOD_STATE$ = $night$
			:i $TODManager_SetTODInstant$$night$
			:i $set_current_tod_values$$tod_state$ = $night$
			:i endcase
		case $morning$
			:i $Change$$LEVEL_TOD_STATE$ = $morning$
			:i $TODManager_SetTODInstant$$morning$
			:i $set_current_tod_values$$tod_state$ = $morning$
			:i endcase
		case $evening$
			:i $Change$$LEVEL_TOD_STATE$ = $evening$
			:i $TODManager_SetTODInstant$$evening$
			:i $set_current_tod_values$$tod_state$ = $evening$
			:i endcase
		default 
			:i $Change$$LEVEL_TOD_STATE$ = $afternoon$
			:i $TODManager_SetTODInstant$$afternoon$
			:i $set_current_tod_values$$tod_state$ = $afternoon$
			:i end_switch
	
	:i $SpawnScript$$thugpro_tod_level_specific_hack_after$
:i endfunction
:i function $thugpro_reset_tod_flags$
	:i $UnsetFlagsExcept$:s{
		:i $flags$ = :a{$SERVER_LEVEL_TOD_NIGHT_ON$$SERVER_LEVEL_TOD_MORNING_ON$$SERVER_LEVEL_TOD_EVENING_ON$:a}
		:i $ex_flag$ = $SERVER_LEVEL_TOD_DAY_ON$
		:i $toggle_flag$
		:i $no_broadcast$
	:i :s}
	:i $Change$$LEVEL_TOD_STATE$ = $afternoon$
:i endfunction
:i function $thugpro_update_tod$
	:i $thugpro_change_time_of_day$$tod_state$ =  ($LEVEL_TOD_STATE$) 
:i endfunction
:i function $thugpro_menu_change_tod$
	:i if $InNetGame$
		:i if NOT $OnServer$
			:i return
			
		:i endif
	:i endif
	:i if NOT $InNetGame$
		:i $wait$%i(2,00000002)$gameframes$
		:i $THUGPRO_SetLightUpdateState$$unpause$
	:i endif
	:i $thugpro_change_time_of_day$$tod_state$ = %GLOBAL%$state$
	:i if $InNetGame$
		:i $Server_BroadcastTOD$$tod_state$ = %GLOBAL%$state$
	:i endif
	:i if NOT $InNetGame$
		:i $wait$%i(60,0000003c)$gameframes$
		:i $THUGPRO_SetLightUpdateState$$pause$
	:i endif
:i endfunction
:i function $thugpro_tod_level_specific_hack_before$
:i endfunction
:i function $thugpro_tod_level_specific_hack_after$
	:i if $LevelIs$$load_ba$
		:i $SpawnScript$$thugpro_BA_ReCreateBridgeParts$
	:i endif
	:i if $LevelIs$$Load_FL$
		:i $THUGPRO_SafeKill$$name$ = $BRIDGEMOVE_01$
		:i $THUGPRO_ForceCreate$$name$ = $BRIDGEMOVE_01$
		:i $THUGPRO_SafeKill$$name$ = $BRIDGEMOVE_02$
		:i $THUGPRO_ForceCreate$$name$ = $BRIDGEMOVE_02$
	:i endif
	:i if $LevelIs$$load_z_sm$
		:i if  ( ($LEVEL_TOD_STATE$)  = $afternoon$) 
			:i $Kill$$prefix$ = %s(12,"Z_SM_NightOn")
		:i endif
	:i endif
:i endfunction
